 If you have a gun or pistol license, you should also understand when your license can be revoked
 
 
 
 
 
 
 1
 If the administration feels that the cancellation of the license of a gun or pistol is necessary for the public interest and safety, it can cancel it
 2
 If a person who has received a gun or pistol license is mentally disturbed, the administration revokes his license
 3
 If someone has obtained a license by giving false information or hiding any information, ie, violating the rules, then such license can be revoked
 4
 a license can be revoked even if there is a violation of the terms of the license, the Arms Act and the Law of Arms Rules
 5
 If the weapon is instructed to be deposited and the licensee fails to comply with it, action can be taken to revoke the license
 6
 If the person has a license, he can cancel his license by applying
 7
 If the High Court finds violation of the Arms Law, it can revoke the license even using its powers
 8
 The license of arms can also be revoked on Central Government directive
 9
 If someone is convicted by the court under the Arms Act or Arms Rules, his license can be revoked

 The Unique Identification Authority of India (UIDAI) states that it does not and will not keep any information related to the bank accounts, health, financial or property of Aadhaar holders
 uske database menadharawalon kii aisi koi jaankaree nahin he
 Selected Information We have the authority said in a public notice that it has little information related to the base holders, which also contains select demographic information

 1
 Hanuman Garhi is the king of Hanuman Garhi temple of Ayodhya Ayodhya
 yahaan kii manyata he ki mandir main jabahanuman ji kii aaratihoti he, us samay vardaan maangane vaale kii har ichha puri hoti he

 tabhi se wo hanumangadhi main virajman ho gayi
